\item 
\#define \hyperlink{parrot_8h_a073ec1e277b3d058a124e241c473d5ee}{H\+A\+V\+E\+\_\+\+E\+N\+U\+M\+\_\+\+M\+A\+V\+\_\+\+C\+MD}
\begin{DoxyCompactList}\small\item\em Commands to be executed by the M\+AV. They can be executed on user request, or as part of a mission script. If the action is used in a mission, the parameter mapping to the waypoint/mission message is as follows\+: Param 1, Param 2, Param 3, Param 4, X\+: Param 5, Y\+:Param 6, Z\+:Param 7. This command list is similar what A\+R\+I\+NC 424 is for commercial aircraft\+: A data format how to interpret waypoint/mission data. \end{DoxyCompactList}\item 
\#define \hyperlink{parrot_8h_a1577e08d90fde759995ea7e5d7033908}{H\+A\+V\+E\+\_\+\+E\+N\+U\+M\+\_\+\+M\+A\+V\+\_\+\+V\+I\+E\+W\+\_\+\+M\+O\+D\+E\+\_\+\+T\+Y\+PE}
\begin{DoxyCompactList}\small\item\em Type of the view mode. This is how the vehicle should behave to set its orientation. \end{DoxyCompactList}\item

\subsection{Detailed Description}
M\+A\+V\+Link comm protocol generated from parrot.\+xml.

\subsection{Macro Definition Documentation}
\index{parrot.\+h@{parrot.\+h}!H\+A\+V\+E\+\_\+\+E\+N\+U\+M\+\_\+\+M\+A\+V\+\_\+\+C\+MD@{H\+A\+V\+E\+\_\+\+E\+N\+U\+M\+\_\+\+M\+A\+V\+\_\+\+C\+MD}}
\index{H\+A\+V\+E\+\_\+\+E\+N\+U\+M\+\_\+\+M\+A\+V\+\_\+\+C\+MD@{H\+A\+V\+E\+\_\+\+E\+N\+U\+M\+\_\+\+M\+A\+V\+\_\+\+C\+MD}!parrot.\+h@{parrot.\+h}}
\subsubsection[{\texorpdfstring{H\+A\+V\+E\+\_\+\+E\+N\+U\+M\+\_\+\+M\+A\+V\+\_\+\+C\+MD}{HAVE_ENUM_MAV_CMD}}]{\setlength{\rightskip}{0pt plus 5cm}\#define H\+A\+V\+E\+\_\+\+E\+N\+U\+M\+\_\+\+M\+A\+V\+\_\+\+C\+MD}\hypertarget{parrot_8h_a073ec1e277b3d058a124e241c473d5ee}{}\label{parrot_8h_a073ec1e277b3d058a124e241c473d5ee}


Commands to be executed by the M\+AV. They can be executed on user request, or as part of a mission script. If the action is used in a mission, the parameter mapping to the waypoint/mission message is as follows\+: Param 1, Param 2, Param 3, Param 4, X\+: Param 5, Y\+:Param 6, Z\+:Param 7. This command list is similar what A\+R\+I\+NC 424 is for commercial aircraft\+: A data format how to interpret waypoint/mission data.

Type of the view mode. This is how the vehicle should behave to set its orientation.
